 is chunaav main congress tathaa basapa ne dimple ke viruddh ummidavaar khadey nahin kiye, jabaki antim kshan main chunaav ladane kaa faisla karne vaali bhaajapa kaa ummidavaar samay rahete namakan karne se chook gaye
 On June 9, Dimple was declared elected unopposed after her name was withdrawn by the United Samajwadi Party candidate Dasaratha Shankhawar and Independent candidate Sanju Katiyar
 naagarikta sanshodhan bill loksabhaa main paas ho chukaa he
 The Lok Sabha has 334 votes in favor of this bill and only 106 against it
 aap kah sakate hai ki sadan main yah bill vyapak aam sahmati se paas hua
 But there does not appear to be a broad consensus in the northeastern states about this bill
 darasal purvottar ke rajyon ke saansadon ko sankhya kam hone ke kaaran bahut baad main or bahut kam samay mila

 Lalrozanga of Mizo National Front, the only MP from Mizoram, supported the bill but the urge cannot be ignored
 lalaroxanga ne kaha ki is bill ko lekar mizoram maansik yatnaa ke daur se guzar rahaa tha
 But the Prime Minister and the Home Minister kept our concerns in mind
 mizoram ko is bill se baahar rakhaa gaya he
 The bill speaks of citizenship on the basis of religious persecution
 ham centre or desh kii sabhi rajya sarkaron se aagrah karte hai ki ve yah sunishchat karen ki kam se kam hamaare yahaan dharmik pratadna na ho
 Whatever assurances have been given about the North East should be fulfilled
 sikikm se bhi ek hi saansad hai
 Indra Hung Subba, MP from Sikkam Employees Front, opposed the bill and said in 1975 that Sikkim was merged with India
 sikkim ke logon kii naagarikta sikkim subjects regulation 1961 ke hisaab se tay hoti he
 The people of Sikkim born before the merger are considered Sikkimese Indians
 unhen naagarikta sanshodhan bill ke daayre se baahar rakhaa janaa chahie tha
 We oppose it
 amit shah ne jawaab main kaha he ki sikkim ko anuchhed 371 ke tahat jo sangrakshan hasil he usase chhedchhad nahin hogi
 There are eight states in the Northeast where this bill will not be fully implemented or will be implemented, in part
 yani virodh kii unki vaazib chintaaon kaa raashtra hit ke virodh main baat sakate hai? is bill ke kaaran pehali baar manipur main inner line permit kii vyavastha laai jaaegi taaki vahaan par naagarikta kanoon lagu na ho sake
 Why a country had to promise an Inner Line Permit to bring this bill, it is important for a country-law-minded people to know
 bagair permit ke koi bhi bhartiya naagarik inner line permit vaale rajyon main na to ja saktaa he or na thahar saktaa he
 Arunachal Pradesh, Mizoram and Nagaland had this system and now the Modi government has promised to implement the Inner Line Permit in Manipur as well, only then Manipur will be kept out of the purview of the citizenship law
 yah purvottar kii zarurat he
 Other border areas of India also have an Inner Line Permit System
 kashmir, ladakh, uttarakhand or himachal pradesh ke sarhad se lage ilaakon main he
 This law is a legacy of the 1873 English law
 2019 main pehali baar manipur main lagu kiya jayega
 People who will get citizenship of India under the new citizenship law cannot settle in Manipur, Mizoram, Nagaland and Arunachal Pradesh
 unhen permit lekar janaa hoga
 What is the stand regarding NRC ie Citizenship Register in North Eastern states
